-- Sec

-- Decryption function
local function decryptScript(encryptedString)
    local decoded = {}
    for char in encryptedString:gmatch("%d+") do
        table.insert(decoded, string.char(tonumber(char)))
    end
    return table.concat(decoded)
end

-- Helper function to securely load the script
local function secureLoadScript(url)
    local success, result = pcall(function()
        local scriptContent = game:HttpGet(url)
        if scriptContent and #scriptContent > 0 then
            loadstring(scriptContent)()
        else
            error("Script content is invalid or empty.")
        end
    end)
    if not success then
        warn("Failed to load script:", result)
        game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
            Title = "Script Error",
            Text = "Failed to load the script. Check your internet connection or contact support.",
            Duration = 5
        })
    end
end
